9  FQ&A 
 
• How high can a mezzanine be? 
The height of the mezzanine is based on the simulation of the reach of the handling 
robots and enough space for when a robot or station needs to be removed, it is worth 
mentioning that the higher the height, the higher the cost. 
 
• How much space should be left between the controllers above the mezzanine 
for walking? 
The length and width of the aisles of the platform will depend on the number of 
controllers and equipment to be integrated. There must be enough space to handle 
the controllers and to avoid other risks. 1m is recommended, although it must be 
validated by Maintenance and EH&S. 
 
• What is the maximum weight capacity that a Mezzanine can support? 
It may vary depending on the number of items to be mounted and of the structure 
itself, so it is recommended to first determine the number (considering your weights) 
and discuss it with the mezzanine integrator so that your design will support the 
desired weight. 
 
• Can ladders or spiral staircases be used? 
Metalsa recommends not to use ladders or spiral staircases, but only conventional 
stairs. However, if the layout situation requires it, ladders can be added to the 
mezzanine, in addition to the main stairway. The ladder can only be used/placed, if 
the EH&S team is aware and agrees, as this entails additional training and 
maintenance costs to be able to use them. 
 
• Can ladders or spiral staircases be used as emergency exits? 
No, they cannot be used as emergency exits from the mezzanine, only the 
“conventional” stairways and the orientation of these must point towards the nearest 
emergency exit of the building. 
 
• Can a fence be placed instead of a handrail or a guardrail on the mezzanine? 
No, OSHA is very clear that it must be a handrail or guardrail with certain 
characteristics. Consult here the section where these characteristics are discussed. 
 
• Do you have to have more than 2 accesses to the mezzanine? 
This will depend primarily on the mezzanine area and layout conditions. 
 
• Is a material access door to the mezzanine necessary? 
This will be defined by the Maintenance and EH&S team; in the first instance it is 
intended that all equipment will be placed above the mezzanine and will not have to 
be removed from its place. In the event that it is deemed necessary, this access must 
comply with the requirements outlined by OSHA in the guardrail section. 

 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
• Does the mezzanine have to be painted in a specific color?  
OSHA states that only those objects to mark physical hazards such as: Striking 
against, stumbling, falling, tripping, and "caught in between" should be painted 
YELLOW. So, the recommendation would be that the edge of the stair tread(s), the 
toe board, handrails, guardrails, and a section of each mezzanine column (impact 
protection is sufficient) should be painted yellow. 
 
Click here to consult the OSHA Standard about:  
Safety color code for marking physical hazards.  
(Standard Number: 1910.144) 
 
• How would the color of the rest of the mezzanine structure be defined? 
Depend on the color of the ship or is it at your discretion, only the yellow color of the 
OSHA elements must be respected. 
 
• What kind of lighting equipment should be in the mezzanine? 
The lighting equipment will be determined according to the standards of the 
infrastructure team in conjunction with EH&S of each line, as the conditions of each 
line may vary. Cold light LED is recommended 
 
• Do the cable trays go outside or inside the mezzanine? 
The recommendation is to go above the mezzanine in an elevated way (similar to 
the arrangement you have with the cells), this to avoid the electrification of the 
structure. 
 
• Will the mezzanine be evaluated by a risk assessment? 
Based on the calculation reports submitted by the supplier, it must be verified and 
certified by a third party that the structure is safe, at least twice the planned weight. 
 
• Does the removable guardrail have to be identified in any way? 
It is recommended to identify it with black stripes or any other type of visual 
difference. 
• Is this standard retroactive to past Metalsa projects? 
Modifications to the structures will be determined by each plant and project. 
However, best safe practices for their use should be followed. 
 
• Do the guidelines presented in this standard apply to the design and best 
practices all mezzanines? 
Modifications to the structures will be determined by each plant and project. 
However, best safe practices for their use should be followed.

Purpose 
The purpose of this document is to establish the criteria with which a projection station 
must comply to ensure its effectiveness and safety. 
 
Introduction 
In this document you will find the requirements to be fulfilled by the screening machine, 
tooling, nut feeder, and services. These criteria must be considered when 
quoting/defining for future projects. 
 
Objective 
The objective of the standard is to ensure the proper operation of the machine on the 
floor, in addition to ensuring the quality of the equipment that Metalsa purchases for 
the assembly lines.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
 
1. Projection Welding  
 
 
 
Suppliers for América: WTC, DENGENSHA, SERRA, CENTERLINE 
 
Use the next information to define what is the best equipment option to use: 
 
➢ When projection ring is presented on HSS/AHSS or UHSS materials with thicknesses 
above 3 mm use CD equipment 
 
➢ Bigger rods for force controls when welding HSS / AHSS or UHSS, these materials 
require bigger forces.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
 
1.1. Types of projection welding machines 
Metalsa considers 2 types of pedestals/Projection Welding Machines (Manual and 
automatic). These pedestals can be single or multi-electrode. (Be able to make the 
projection 1 to N times at the same time at the same station.)  
 
MANUAL PEDESTAL WELDER 
This type of pedestals is used by an operator, they can be fixed electrode or 
multi-electrode. 
 
AUTOMATIC PEDESTAL WELDER  
It is a pedestal that needs to be integrated into a robotic cell, requiring a material 
handling robot, a material preloading station, and a material discharge station, in 
addition to the pedestal itself. 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Automatic 
1 Electrode 
Manual 
Multi-electrode 
Manual 
1 Electrode

3. Capacities & requirements of the transformer & 
controller   
 
3.1. Transformer  
The controller supplier must include the transformer according to the application 
requirements.  
 
All welding transformers for new projects in Metalsa must have a 50% extra capacity 
than the required according to calculations based on the thickness of the materials that 
to be welded.  
Calculations are responsibility of the resistance welding equipment supplier. During buy 
off / weld view Metalsa must corroborate that the equipment transformer fulfills the 
requirement of 50 % extra capacity, integrator must deliver calculation study. 
 
3.2 
Controller 
The medium frequency controller offers a flexible and intuitive programming for the 
personalization of the welding process.  
 
There are different sizes of inverters for the generation of high currents of welding.   
 
➢ 400 AMPS 
➢ 1200 AMPS 
➢ 2400 AMPS

4. Tooling (GD&T Definition) 
 
In order for the supplier to be able to design and manufacture the tooling, it is 
necessary that the project team provides technical drawings of the parts to be welded 
(2D and 3D) together with the torque and push out specifications. 
 
The main purpose of this section is to describe the method to align the components 
tolerances to the weld process and how each component is located in the assembly 
fixture.  
 
This activity should be performed by the project teams before the definition of stamping 
parts processes (The design agreed by VP must be followed according to the quotation). 
 
The design and construction of the tooling must be based on the NAAMS standard. 
 
 
 
NOTES:  
• Validate that the tooling allows for easy loading and unloading of the part 
• Pre-loading stations must ensure part stability 
• The electrode must be flat

4.3 
Insulation on the secondary circuit  
 
Projection welding stations 
The part register block must be made of steel (A36) and the screws must be insulated 
from the tower, and the tower must be insulated from the base plate with Micartra, 
Nylamid or Celeron. 
 
Robot wrist (For automated projection stations requiring material handling robots) 
Robot wrist must be isolated when a gripper is used to hold a part while is being welded 
by another equipment. Robot holding a spot-welding gun must be isolated also from this 
point. 
o Celoron 
o Nylamid 
o Micarta 
 

 
16 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
4.3.1 Screws in secondary circuit  
Screws at the secondary circuit where there is a current flow must be made of 
austenitic stainless steel in order to avoid magnetic fields in the circuit  
 
The screws must be millimetric (M6, M8 and M10). The metric system must be used for 
the manufacturing of the tooling, and stainless socket screws must be used. 
 
Validate that the material registers (screws) have access for adjustment, reference Allen 
wrench (50 mm wrench height).

✓ It's required a stainless-steel bushing for protection of the lower 
electrode in weld projection for bolts applications.

4.5 
Poka-Yokes 
The purpose of this section is to ensure since the verification of the product and process 
design, take the necessary actions to design prevention systems that helps to reduce the 
dependency on the operator for the detection of the possible defects during the 
product transformation. 
 
The registration of the pieces must ensure that the piece is placed only in the correct 
position (Mechanical Pokayoke) 
 
▪ This style of Poka-Yoke is a combination between a good product and process 
design. 
▪ i.e.  Hole in the parts oriented to the same direction, allows to have fixed pin in the 
tool to prevent a part misplaced or mixed. 
 
▪ Mechanical and inductive sensor for holes present. 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

 
21 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
4.5.1 Detection Devices  
All projection welding machines used in the Metalsa process must be equipped with a 
system capable to detect in the electrode and feeding system the following conditions 
must be included on projection welding workstations for nuts:  
• Part misloaded  
• Upside down nut condition  
• Misalignment between nut and part diameter 
• Missing nut  
• Missing part  
  
 
In addition, in order to meet the requirements of Industry 4.0, the station must be 
equipped with the ANDON system capable of alerting when a quality check of torque or 
change of consumables must be made

4.5.2 LPT  
The BTL6 Micropulse Transducer, together with a machine controller (e.g. PLC), comprises 
a position measuring system. It is intended to be installed into a machine or system.

5. Heat Sink system  
5.1. Flow and water requirements 
 
The water flow requirements for the resistance welding equipment are the following 
(minimum values): 
 
• Total circuit flow must be at least 15 liters per minutes 
• If the welding controller is water – cooled, and extra 1 GPM in the circuit is needed. 
Note: It is important to check the specifications of the total circuit flow because 
some of them might need more flow.  
 
The quality and properties of the water must follow the RWMA specification 5-005.05 at 
all times. The maximum inlet temperature should not exceed 86°F (30°C) or fall 
below the dew point of the ambient air at about 59°F (15°C).  
Additional cooling tubes in the welding gun must comply with the standard. BIW-F-
Palletized-09-002 (Cut at 45 ° and 3mm below adapter stop). 
 
1. Maximum pressure not to exceed 90 PSI 
2. pH maintained between 7.0 and 8.0 
3. Maximum chloride content 20 parts per million (PPM) 
4. Maximum nitrate content 10 PPM 
5. Maximum sulfate content 100 PPM 
6. Maximum suspended solids content 100 PPM, non-abrasive 
7. Maximum total (suspended and dissolved) solids content 250 PPM 
8. Maximum calcium carbonate content 250 PPM 
9. Resistivity less than 2,000 ohms/cm at 25° C. (500 mS) 
10. The hose used must be NO LESS THAN 18 in. long across the 
11. power voltages. 
 
Note: Water that is safe for drinking is generally sufficient for cooling water, provided it is 
filtered to eliminate sand and rust particles. In addition, water temperature must NOT fall 
more than 2. C. below the temperature of the surrounding air.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
5.2.1 Heat sink devices 
Cooling systems 
 
 
 
NOTE: The material for the Exchanger-Towers water system is PVC  
 
 
 

 
25 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
The system used in the 18PL line is a hybrid of open circuit of exchanger tower and closed 
system, the way that the team define the cooling method is different for each case, an 
analysis of the life cycle of the system is the important for taking the decision also the 
costs of energy that it takes, the recommendation is that in cases where there are about 
10 machines the best option would be a mini-chiller but when there are 40 or 50 
machines the best option would be an exchanger Tower.  
 
This hybrid system also is the best option for no having contamination in the water that 
is in the cooling system. Also, the equipment of welding projection is not that sensible to 
the variation of temperature, and that´s why is not precise to have a closed system.  
Recommended brands: 
 
 
Exchanger tower Model recommended: RTU-7UB175-A 
 
Exchanger   
For getting more information about the cooling systems (INFRA/ Specifications of service 
pipes): KC Infrastructure - Infra Especificaciones Tuberias de Servicio R0 20may22.pdf - All 
Documents (sharepoint.com) (Especificar seccion)

6. Safety & Ergonomics 
Stations of projection welding must include the following in order to be safety 
approved: 
 
1. Risk Assessment 
A preliminary risk assessment and risk reduction based on current revision of ANSI B11.0 
Safety of Machinery Safety of machinery shall be conducted and presented to Metalsa 
EHS and Engineering teams, machine builder must obtain written acceptance from both 
prior to building equipment. This risk assessment shall be used determine the 
performance level and category required for the safety related parts of the control 
system.  
 
2. Light Curtains 
A pair light curtains 800mm. Must be covers with guards to protect them from impacts. 
(Metalsa recommends using BANNER or SICK brand).  
 
All Light curtains shall be selected (SICK or BANNER brand, specific model to be 
approved by Metalsa at design review) and located at the operator loading access to the 
station, Light curtains shall be selected and installed with strict adherence to the current 
revision of ISO 13855  
 
Photo of Center Line's Flex Fast Lite Station 
 
 

 
27 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
3. Fence 
The station should have fence (As well as all the guards) to prevent an operator or any 
third party from getting too close to the station. Polycarbonate may also an acceptable 
material (provided meets the requirements of the standards and is agreed upon with 
Metalsa) in lieu of fence all guarding shall meet and be installed in compliance with the 
requirements of the current revision ISO 14120, any other material must be consulted 
and approved by Metalsa. 
 
4. Fan (Optional) 
In case the station does not have its own fan, consider the (Model WI-30 Brisa or 
Schaefer 30" OSHA Compliant Circulation Fan 30” CFO-B, 115V) Should be mounted at a 
height of approximately 215 cm from the floor. Provides air for 2-3 stations (Must be 
validated before) 
 
5. Light Operator 
The station must have an illumination in the work area of 300 lux minimum, for more 
information see the lighting standard for workstations (click here). The position of the 
lamp will depend on the conditions of each place where the station is placed, just make 
sure that it does not disturb the operator and the operation. 
 
6. LOTO 
Control of Hazardous Energy Lockout, Tagout, and Alternative Methods. All Metalsa 
equipment shall have a means of ensuring safety of all parties when working with 
equipment, preventing unexpected energization or start-up of the equipment or an 
unexpected release of stored energy. Through LOTO or use of alternative means when 
allowed based on a completed risk assessment. All hazardous energy control shall be 
implemented in accordance with the current revision of ANSI/ASSE Z244.1. The 
equipment supplier shall provide a written procedure with pictograms and step-by-step 
task to complete energy isolation. Hazardous energy lockout shall eliminate the 
possibility of all actions of person(s) from resulting in harm when performing both 
routine and non-routine task while LOTO is in place. 
 
NOTES: 
• The station must have a safe method for the electrodes to be aligned, the alignment 
must be by means of the pass-through test (The test must be performed once a 
week, validated by the maintenance team). 
• The station must be able to run cycle without projection (dry run), This setting can 
only be activated by an authorized person and from the HMI.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
7. Emergency Stop Function 
Equipment shall have an emergency stop function in compliance to current revisions of 
ISO 13850 
 
 
8. Resistance Welding Safety. 
All resistance welding equipment shall be selected for safe application to the work 
intended. The personnel safety aspects of resistance welding shall be given consideration 
when choosing equipment for the work to be performed and comply with safety norms 
from each region where Metalsa facilities are located. For further details, refer to MAKC 
Safety Requirements Manual in MOS Portal. 
 
Compliance to OSHA 1910.255 titled Resistance Welding and ANSI B11.0 and all other 
applicable standards included in 10 - Safety Global Requirements V11.0.pdf must be 
met. 
 
9. Final Risk Assessment 
An as built risk assessment and risk reduction based on current revision of ANSI B11.0 
Safety of Machinery Safety of machinery shall be conducted and presented to Metalsa 
EHS and Engineering teams at equipment runoff, the machine builder must obtain 
written acceptance and ok to ship from both teams prior to shipment. 
Please note adherence to ANSI B11.0 ensures compliance to ISO 12100; however 
following ISO 12100 does not ensure compliance to B11.0.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
7. Peripheral systems 
7.1. Nut Feeder 
The feeder must ensure that the nut size and orientation are 
correct 
• Automatic nut feeder for projection welding stations  
• Manual nut or bolt feeding is not allowed. 
• Must include cover 
• Maximal distance 6 meters from feeder to rod, avoid hose 
bends, curvatures through hose must allowed nut to travel 
freely.  
• Feeder must be anchored and leveled (Important) 
*This equipment shall be according to brands selected for 
projection welding detailed at the beginning of this manual. 
The degree of vibration should be between 3 and 4 Hz 
 
 
 
7.2.1 Detection Poka-Yoke (Preferential) 
Nut Feeder nut size detection and correct orientation of the nut. The equipment must 
have an encoder to detect the correct part is assembled. 
 
Also, the hose must have a poka-yoke to prevent it from being disconnected and 
connected backwards, causing the nut to be placed incorrectly. 
 
 
 
Guide to discard

Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
7.2.2 Automatic nut and bolt feeders (mandatory) 
• Automatic nut feeder for projection welding stations  
• Manual nut or bolt feeding is not allowed. 
o Must include cover 
o (Maximal distance 6 meters from feeder to rod), avoid hose bends, curvatures 
through hose must allowed nut to travel freely.  
o Feeder must be fixed (Important) 
*This equipment shall be according to brands selected for projection welding detailed at 
the beginning of this manual. 
 
7.2.   Air Supply  
System requires as minimum pressure 80 PSI, and the calibration for the optimal 
pressure for the nuts will be through the regulator.

8. Equipment for current, voltage and force 
measurement. 
Consider at least one equipment that helps you measure at least the real amount of 
current, voltage, time and force applied, this will be used during design of experiments 
for weld schedules and parameters audit.  
 
 1.- Weld Analyzer 
Capable of measuring (some of the next characteristics, 
as minimum): 
• 
AC and MF DC welding current 
• 
The number of pulses in the weld 
• 
Duration of each weld 
• 
Voltage 
• 
Resistance 
• 
Power 
 
Devices must include 
• Flexible coil for current measurement 
• Voltage sensors 
• Traceable calibration certificate 
• May also be capable to connected to a computer to extend its storage capabilities 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 
Analyzer for visual aid only 

 
34 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
 
2.- Weld Probe Force Gage 
The force Gage is an instrument able to measure the force between two points, in this 
case, way to use it is between the electrodes and closing them disabling first the 
welding. 
 
 
Capable of measuring up to 3,000 lbf (13,350 Newtons) 
 
 
3.- Torque meter 
This is used to measure the torque force required to remove a nut.

Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
 
4.- Hand-Weld Scope  
This instrument provides a variety of monitoring equipment, including weld scopes and 
pressure sensor to ensure accurate current/pressure monitoring, and recording of weld 
quality, weld scopes can measure welding current, cycle time and peak current.

9. Consumables 
9.1. Projection welding electrodes 
The deterioration of the electrodes is less than in spot welding since there is less heat 
generated and the heat and wear are distributed over a larger area. Upper electrode must 
be 15% bigger than nut to be welded. 
 
For this process, it is recommended that the material of the electrode that will be facing 
the surface of the base material to be a Cupper + Tungsten Alloy (CuW) “Elkonite ®” 
and the rest of the body of the electrode class 2. It is important that the joint of these 
inserts is welded and not threaded in order to avoid internal ark strikes. 
 
 
 
RWMA Class 2 (Tungsten 75% – Copper 25%) 
Is recommended as facing inserts for flash and butt-welding dies and general-purpose projection 
welding electrodes. 
 
 
In the case of Europe use either electrodes class 2 or 20 for projection welding. 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

 
37 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
9.2. Projection Welding locator pins (CONSUMIBLES) 
Used to guide the nut and guide it through the bottom electrode to sit on it, there are a 
lot of pins shapes regarding the size and shape of the nut, and different kind of alloys 
regarding the use (Ceramic, Stainless steel, Zircon and Alumina).  
 
Refer to supplier suggestion, to match the best according to your application. 
 
 
 
9.2.1 PLP Pin Design requirements 
Locating Pins 
 All locating pins will be SAE 8620 steel or equivalent. Hardened to Rockwell C- 58-62 to 
a depth of .5 mm -2.0 mm- NAAMS (North American Automotive Metric Standard) pin 
locators are preferred. 
 
PLP Locating Pins Extension Through Gage Holes  
PLP locating pins should extend through the gage holes a minimum length of 5mm and 
a maximum of 10mm, not including taper lead. 
 
 

 
38 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
Datum Hole Design Requirements 
 
 
 
a) Inside thread:  
For holder pilot type NAAMS 
b) Shoulder mount:  
To pilot holder with setting 
c) With Barrette:  
Pilot lateral holder for towers 
(web rail registration) 
 
 
Option 1: 
• Material: SAE 8620 steel  
• Thermal treatment: Cemented with a hardness of 58-62 RC. 0.7mm depth after 
rectified 0.5 
• Finish: Black oxide. 
• Specification: The design of the pilots must be common as they are used in the 
same reference. 
• The design of all pins must have a non-rotating plane. 
• Add:  a mark on the pilot body to monitor its wear. 
• This mark will be of 0.5mm of depth depending on it is four or two- ways 
• The orientation of the mark must be subject to the contact piece. 

 
39 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
Option 2:  
• Material: M-2 58-62 RC 
• Specification: The design of the pilots must be common as they are used in the 
same reference. 
• The design of all pins must have a non-rotating plane. 
• No line mark needed 
 
Note:  
The selection of the pins is left to the integrator following the specifications of the 
GD&T 
 
 
9.2. Shunt 
Are meant to transfer the weld current from the transformer to the secondary circuit 
without generate heat to the circuit. 
There are two option to use for shunt: 
• Laminated  
• Braid cables 
      
 
Shape and hole pattern, it is responsibility of supplier according to equipment design. 
When a specific workpiece requires amperages above 20,000 amps or the distance 
between connections is longer that 30 cm, use braid cable as shunt since there are 
conductivity advantages and longer lifetime, this type of braid cables provide less 
resistance and less temperature. 
 
Shunt resistance must be documented before using the equipment, preventive 
maintenance practices during production will require to replace the shunt if the resistance 
is 20% above the original resistance previously documented. 
 
 
 
 
 
 
 

 
40 
 
 
Copyright © Metalsa, S.A. de C.V. Carretera Miguel Alemán Km. 16.5 No. 100, Apodaca Nuevo León, México, 66600. 2017 
Complete or partial reproduction of this material is prohibited without the owner’s explicit consent. 
 
10. Quality check  
10.2 Projections welding Quality Check 
To release any new equipment must be run at least 30 pcs, for each kind of nut, all must 
be into the customer spec. 
 
 
11. Layout Station 
It is essential that the team that designs the arrangement of the stations along with the 
material containers in the layout of the line/project considers the handling of the 
part/product by the operator. 
 
The arrangement of the station and the material containers must allow the operator: 
• Access the station easily (Avoid having the station in narrow places) 
• Manage the parts easily (Loading and unloading)

1 Purpose 
This document has the intention to define and clarify the guidelines to be considering for 
robot model selection based on process and product considerations. 
2 Introduction 
These guidelines are the standard that all projects must follow in order to be more 
Competitive and reduce the initial CAPEX Investment.  
3 Objective 
The objective is to provide criterial in order to ensure the best robot selection since the 
process design conceptualization. 
 
 
 
 
The evidence to ensure the fulfillment of the guidelines stablished in this standard will be 
evaluate through the Process Verification Workshop.



 
Tools design characteristics to facilitate weld access. (indexer table, trunnion 
fixture) 
 
 
Quantity of robots per tool.
